	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') != 'e02615d6f7a198f55289e38c71b53ae4720aad12') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== 'e02615d6f7a198f55289e38c71b53ae4720aad12') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== 'f753745118dcc2bf6278a8fd06c956eb00437f1f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== 'e02615d6f7a198f55289e38c71b53ae4720aad12') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/oidplus_base.js')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/oidplus_base.js');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('includes/oidplus_base.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/oidplus_base.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') != 'ae730a2dbadc2ce92b6e71de1e0bed53859c3253') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus_base.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/oidplus_base.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/oidplus_base.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') !== 'ae730a2dbadc2ce92b6e71de1e0bed53859c3253') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') !== 'ab4585a62e1714ac305f233ca07f89b29c93f4c7') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/oidplus_base.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/oidplus_base.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/oidplus_base.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/oidplus_base.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') !== 'ae730a2dbadc2ce92b6e71de1e0bed53859c3253') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus_base.js');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/oidplus_functions.js')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/oidplus_functions.js');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('includes/oidplus_functions.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/oidplus_functions.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/oidplus_functions.js') != 'cbad3c3d201aff8207184b2dbca62809d0e9fa78') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus_functions.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/oidplus_functions.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/oidplus_functions.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_functions.js') !== 'cbad3c3d201aff8207184b2dbca62809d0e9fa78') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_functions.js') !== 'dbc8536fbbef4f176e96b05810e8c219ca0f3b0c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/oidplus_functions.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/oidplus_functions.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/oidplus_functions.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/oidplus_functions.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_functions.js') !== 'cbad3c3d201aff8207184b2dbca62809d0e9fa78') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus_functions.js');
		}
	}
}
